# Degree Candidates Announced
## 963 Students Will Receive June Degrees 
### 
Candidates for baccalaureate
degrees this June numbered 963
as of noon last Tuesday, accord
ing to the Registrar's Office.
Included on the list are the fol
lowing students. Officials stress
that this list includes only those
who have filed for degrees in
June.

Candidates for baccalaureate
degrees this June numbered 963
as of noon last Tuesday, accord
ing to the Registrar's Office.
Included on the list are the fol
lowing students. Officials stress
that this list includes only those
who have filed for degrees in
June.
